! Some adjectival lexica, the main part of them is found in the
! file sme-lex.txt

LEXICON LEXATTR  ! This lexicon is here to give the tags to the compounding
+A+Attr:%> ATTR ; ! attributive forms.

LEXICON At !NB Have commented out everything except K ; here to avoid strange
          ! compounds like -šlailágán etc. Attr. that can be compounded with
          ! NAMAT etc are redirected to LEXATTR
+A+Attr:%> K ;
+A+Attr: RHyph ;
!+A+Attr-:#%- ProperNoun ;   ! Compounds
!+A+Attr:# AGADJECT ;
!+A+Attr+lágan:lágan LAGAN ; ! Derivation !tentative !
!+A+Attr:# NAMAT ; ! comp-only adj
!+A+Attr:# ALIT ;  ! both comp and independent adj !

LEXICON FINJU- !compounds only
+A+Attr+Use/Sub:%> Rreal ; 
+A+Attr:» NAMAT ;

LEXICON ALIT 								   !
! Both second-part compound and independent adj!
! čáhppesalit bábir							   !
! alit bábir								   !
alit+Use/Circ:alih BEAKKAN ;   ! blue				   !
ruoksat+Use/Circ:ruoks VIELG ; ! red					   !
háváš+Use/Circ:háváž BEAKKAN ; ! -times				   !
stábat+Use/Circ:stábag AGAdj ; !						   !

LEXICON NAMAT
:»»» NAMATCont ;

LEXICON NAMATCont ! second-part compounds
+Der1+Der2+Der/lágan: LAGAN ;
+Der1+Der2+Der/lágaš: LAGAS ;

+Der1+Der2+Der/jagaš+CmpN/SgN+CmpN/PlG:jagaž AGAdj ;

LEXICON Adjective

! Tentative analysis of compulsatory 
! compounds.
bonju FINJU- ;
finju FINJU- ;
vinju FINJU- ;

+Use/Circ: ALIT ; ! adjs that can both stand alone and be ! 
      ! second part of compounds.

! The adjectives themselves
! =========================
